OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 005 ATGLEN
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 005 ATGLEN
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 024 E BRADFORD S-2
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 024 E BRADFORD S-2
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 035 E BRANDYWINE N-1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 035 E BRANDYWINE N-1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 050 CALN 2
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 050 CALN 2
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

DEMOCRATIC 056 EAST CALN 2
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate

elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the

2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 120 COATESVILLE 5
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 120 COATESVILLE 5
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 165 E COVENTRY 2
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 165 E COVENTRY 2
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 195 EASTTOWN 1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 195 EASTTOWN 1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of

subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904

DEMOCRATIC 215 ELK
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 215 ELK
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 243 E GOSHEN 1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 243 E GOSHEN 1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 250 E GOSHEN 8
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 250 E GOSHEN 8
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 265 W GOSHEN M-1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 265 W GOSHEN M-1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 295 HONEY BROOK BOROUGH
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 320 KENNETT TOWNSHIP 1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 320 KENNETT TOWNSHIP 1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of

BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the

for that candidate.

name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.

containing the declaration of the elector to the

statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 365 W MARLBOROUGH
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 365 W MARLBOROUGH
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."

for that candidate.

write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.

for a new ballot.

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 420 OXFORD W
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 420 OXFORD W
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."

INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 463 PHOENIXVILLE N-3
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 463 PHOENIXVILLE N-3
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 477 PHOENIXVILLE W-1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 477 PHOENIXVILLE W-1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 525 W PIKELAND
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 525 W PIKELAND
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 556 SCHUYLKILL 3
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 556 SCHUYLKILL 3
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 581 THORNBURY 2
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 614 TREDYFFRIN M-1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 614 TREDYFFRIN M-1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 654 UWCHLAN 2
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 654 UWCHLAN 2
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 672 VALLEY N-3
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 672 VALLEY N-3
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 693 W VINCENT 2
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 693 W VINCENT 2
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 720 WESTTOWN 1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 720 WESTTOWN 1
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 745 E WHITELAND 3
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 745 E WHITELAND 3
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections

OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 780 WILLISTOWN N-3
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
OFFICIAL GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION BALLOT
DEMOCRATIC 780 WILLISTOWN N-3
COUNTY OF CHESTER, COMMONWEALTH OF PENNSYLVANIA
GENERAL PRIMARY ELECTION - APRIL 23, 2024
INSTRUCTIONS TO VOTER
1. TO VOTE YOU MUST COMPLETELY
BLACKEN THE OVAL ( ) TO THE LEFT OF
YOUR CHOICE. An oval ( ) blackened to the
left of the name of any candidate indicates a vote
for that candidate.
2. To cast a write-in vote for a person whose
name is not on the ballot, you must blacken the
oval ( ) to the left of the line provided, and
write or print the name in the blank space
provided for that purpose.
3. Use only black ink pen.
4. If you make a mistake DO NOT ERASE. Ask
for a new ballot.
5. For Absentee Ballot Voters: "The official
absentee voter ballot shall state that an elector
who receives an absentee ballot pursuant to
section 1301 and whose voted ballot is not timely
received by the commission and who, on Election
Day, is capable of voting at the appropriate
polling place may only vote on Election Day by
provisional ballot unless the elector brings the
elector's absentee ballot to the elector's polling
place, remits the ballot and the envelope
containing the declaration of the elector to the
Judge of Elections to be spoiled and signs a
statement subject to the penalties under 18
PA.C.S. § 4904 (relating to the unsworn
falsification to the authorities) to the same effect."
6. For Mail-in Ballot Voters: "The official mail-in
voter ballot shall state that a voter who receives a
mail-in ballot under section 1301-D and whose
voted mail-in ballot is not timely received may
only vote on Election Day by provisional ballot
unless the elector brings the elector's mail-in
ballot to the elector's polling place, remits the
ballot and the envelope containing the
declaration of the elector to the Judge of
Elections to be spoiled and signs a statement
subject to the penalties of 18 PA.C.S. § 4904
(relating to the unsworn falsification to the
authorities) to the same effect."
Chester County Board of
Elections
